Calculation Trail (every step, every number)
Step 1 — Pi Ratings
formula: composite = (home_rating + away_rating) / 2
Netherlands: home_rating=0.5309, away_rating=-0.0531 → composite = (0.5309 + -0.0531) / 2 = 0.2389 (from 6 matches)
Sweden: home_rating=0.7117, away_rating=-0.0712 → composite = (0.7117 + -0.0712) / 2 = 0.3202 (from 6 matches)
Step 2 — Calibration Parameters
total_anchor = 3.0000 (fitted, n=32 2026 matches)
rho = -0.0300 (fitted) — Dixon-Coles low-score correlation
Step 3 — Lambdas (Expected Goals per Team)
formula: margin = home_composite − away_composite
formula: λ_H = max(0.30, total_anchor/2 + margin/2)
formula: λ_A = max(0.30, total_anchor/2 − margin/2)
margin = 0.2389 − 0.3202 = -0.0813
λ_H = max(0.30, 3.0000/2 + -0.0813/2) = 1.4593
λ_A = max(0.30, 3.0000/2 − -0.0813/2) = 1.5407
Step 4 — Dixon-Coles PMF Grid (26×26)
formula: P(h,a) = τ(h,a,ρ) × Poisson(h; λ_H) × Poisson(a; λ_A), then normalise
τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2
With λ_H=1.4593, λ_A=1.5407, ρ=-0.0300:
τ(0,0) = 1 − 1.4593×1.5407×(-0.0300) = 1.0675
Grid sum = 1.000000 (should be ≈1.000000)
E[home goals] = 1.4593, E[away goals] = 1.5407
Step 5 — Market Derivations (cell summation)
home_win = Σ P(h,a) for h > a = 0.3574
draw = Σ P(h,a) for h = a = 0.2495
away_win = Σ P(h,a) for h < a = 0.3931
over_2.5 = Σ P(h,a) for h+a > 2.5 = 0.5768
btts_yes = Σ P(h,a) for h≥1 AND a≥1 = 0.6065

τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2

formula: P(h,a) = τ(h,a,ρ) × Poisson(h; λ_H) × Poisson(a; λ_A), then normalise
τ(0,0)=1−λ_H×λ_A×ρ, τ(1,0)=1+λ_A×ρ, τ(0,1)=1+λ_H×ρ, τ(1,1)=1−ρ, τ(h,a)=1 for h+a≥2
